date.setTime(date.getTime + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)); const expires = "expires=" + date.toUTCString; document.cookie = `${name}=${value};${expires};path=/`; } function getCookie(name) { const cookies = document.cookie.split(';'); for (let cookie of cookies) { const [cookieName, cookieValue] = cookie.trim.split('='); if (cookieName === name) return cookieValue; } return null; } // ====== THEME TOGGLE ====== const themeToggle = document.createElement('button'); themeToggle.id = 'themeToggle'; themeToggle.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-moon"></i> Dark Mode'; themeToggle.classList.add('theme-button'); themeToggle.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Toggle dark mode'); themeToggle.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-sun"></i> Light Mode'; } else { setCookie('theme', 'light', 30); themeToggle.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-moon"></i> Dark Mode'; } }); // Apply theme on load window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',  => { const theme = getCookie('theme') || 'light'; 'true': 'false'); } } if (!window.__mobileNavInitialized) { window.__mobileNavInitialized = true; if (mobileMenuBtn && mobileNav) { mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleMobileMenu); } if (mobileNavClose && mobileNav) { mobileNavClose.addEventListener('click', toggleMobileMenu); } // Close mobile menu when clicking on a link document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-nav a').forEach(link => { link.addEventListener('click', toggleMobileMenu); }); } // ====== SLIDER FUNCTIONALITY ====== document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function { let currentSlide = 0; const slides = document.querySelectorAll('.slide'); const dots = document.querySelectorAll('.slider-dot'); const slideCount = slides.length; // Preload images to ensure they load properly const imageUrls = [ '/images/executive-protection-services.jpg', '/images/randomized-patrol-schedules.jpg', '/images/customer-and-staff-safety.jpg', '/images/inventory-protection.jpg', '/images/access-control-and-screening.jpg' ]; // Create image elements to preload imageUrls.forEach(url => { const img = new Image; img.src = url; }); function showSlide(index) { // Ensure index is within bounds if (index < 0) index = slideCount - 1; if (index >= slideCount) index = 0; slides.forEach(slide => slide.classList.remove('active')); dots.forEach(dot => dot.classList.remove('active')); slides[index].classList.add('active'); dots[index].classList.add('active'); currentSlide = index; } function nextSlide { let nextIndex = (currentSlide + 1) % slideCount; showSlide(nextIndex); } let slideInterval = setInterval(nextSlide, 5000); dots.forEach(dot => { dot.addEventListener('click', function { let index = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-index')); showSlide(index); clearInterval(slideInterval); slideInterval = setInterval(nextSlide, 5000); }); }); // Pause slider on hover const heroSlider = document.querySelector('.hero-slider'); heroSlider.addEventListener('mouseenter',  => clearInterval(slideInterval)); heroSlider.addEventListener('mouseleave',  => { clearInterval(slideInterval); slideInterval = setInterval(nextSlide, 5000); }); // Add keyboard navigation document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => { if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft') { showSlide(currentSlide - 1); clearInterval(slideInterval); slideInterval = setInterval(nextSlide, 5000); } else if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') { showSlide(currentSlide + 1); clearInterval(slideInterval); slideInterval = setInterval(nextSlide, 5000); } }); }); // ====== HEADER SCROLL EFFECT ====== window.addEventListener('scroll', function { const header = document.querySelector('header'); if (window.scrollY > 50) { header.style.padding = '10px 5%'; header.style.boxShadow = '0 5px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)'; } else { header.style.padding = '15px 5%'; header.style.boxShadow = '0 2px 15px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)'; } }); // ====== SMOOTH SCROLLING ====== document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => { anchor.addEventListener('click', function(e) { e.preventDefault; const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href')); if (target) { window.scrollTo({ top: target.offsetTop - 80, behavior: 'smooth' }); } }); }); // ====== FORM SUBMISSION ====== const contactForm = document.getElementById('web3form'); Transport Vehicle for Cash in Transit Services"> </div> <div class="details-content"> <h3>What is Cash In Transit?</h3> <p>Cash in Transit (CIT) involves the secure transportation of cash, valuables and high-risk items between locations using dedicated vehicles and trained security personnel. This service is essential for banks, retailers, casinos and businesses requiring secure cash logistics.</p> <p>At Broadsafe Services, our cash in transit services follow strict security protocols and utilise dedicated vehicles equipped with GPS tracking, communication systems and advanced safety features. We ensure safe and timely delivery of valuables through secure cash logistics standards.</p> <h3>Key Benefits</h3> <ul class="benefits-list"> <li>Real-time GPS tracking and monitoring</li> <li>Comprehensive incident response planning</li> <li>Secure loading and unloading procedures</li> <li>Insurance coverage for transported items</li> <li>24/7 monitoring and communication</li> <li>Experienced, highly trained security personnel</li> </ul> </div> </div> </section> <!-- Service Features Section --> <section class="service-features"> <div class="section-title"> <h2>Our Cash In Transit Features</h2> <p>Advanced cash movement security solutions for safe transportation of valuables</p> </div> <div class="features-grid"> <div class="feature-card"> <div class="feature-icon"> <i class="fas fa-map-marked-alt"></i> </div> <h3>GPS Tracking</h3> <p>Real-time GPS tracking supported by a 24/7 monitoring centre and route optimisation for secure cash transportation.</p> </div> <div class="feature-card"> <div class="feature-icon"> <i class="fas fa-bolt"></i> </div> <h3>Rapid Response</h3> <p>Immediate emergency response capabilities for high-risk cash transport, with backup teams on standby.</p> </div> <div class="feature-card"> <div class="feature-icon"> <i class="fas fa-headset"></i> </div> <h3>24/7 Communication</h3> <p>Continuous communication with monitoring centre and emergency services coordination for reliable cash handling security.</p> </div> </div> </section> <!-- Security Measures Section --> <section class="security-measures"> <div class="section-title"> <h2>Security Protocols & Measures</h2> <p>Comprehensive security procedures supporting cash in transit solutions</p> </div> <div class="security-container"> <div class="security-content"> <h3>Advanced Security Protocols</h3> <p>Our professional cash in transit service follows stringent security protocols designed to minimise risk and ensure safe transportation. <h1>Construction Site Security Solutions</h1> <p>specialised security services for construction sites to prevent theft, vandalism and ensure safety compliance.</p> <div class="hero-buttons"> <a href="#contact" class="cta-button">Request Site Security Quote</a> </div> </div> </section> <!-- Service Details Section --> <section class="service-details"> <div class="section-title"> <h2>Construction Site Security</h2> <p>Comprehensive security solutions tailored for construction sites and building projects</p> </div> <div class="details-container"> <div class="service-image"> <img src="../images/construction-site-security-services.jpg" alt="Construction Site Security"> </div> <div class="details-content"> <h3>What is Construction Site Security?</h3> <p>Construction site security involves specialised security measures designed to protect construction sites from theft, vandalism, unauthorized access and safety violations. Construction sites are particularly vulnerable due to their open nature, valuable equipment and materials.</p> <p>At Broadsafe Services, we provide comprehensive construction site security solutions that address the unique challenges of building projects. Our services include 24/7 site security personnel, access control systems, perimeter security and safety compliance monitoring.</p> <h3>Key Benefits</h3> <ul class="benefits-list"> <li>24/7 on-site security personnel for continuous protection</li> <li>Access control for workers, visitors and delivery vehicles</li> <li>Theft prevention for tools, equipment and materials</li> <li>Vandalism and trespassing deterrence</li> <li>Safety compliance monitoring and reporting</li> <li>Perimeter security with fencing and lighting</li> <li>Equipment tracking and inventory management</li> <li>Reduced insurance premiums with professional security</li> </ul> </div> </div> </section> <!-- Service Features Section --> <section class="service-features"> <div class="section-title"> <h2>Our Construction As a leading security company, we provide comprehensive solutions including crowd control, access management, emergency response planning and VIP protection services tailored to your specific requirements.</p> <p>At <a href="https://www.broadsafeservices.com.au/">Broadsafe Services</a>, we deliver professional event security guard services that ensure safety and smooth operations. We deploy <a href="staticguarding.html" style="color: var(--primary); text-decoration: underline;">professional static guarding services</a> at entry points, ticket barriers, VIP zones and emergency exits, supported by <a href="mobilepatrols.html" style="color: var(--primary); text-decoration: underline;">mobile patrol security services</a> that move continuously around venue perimeters, car parks, backstage zones and surrounding areas to identify and respond to issues quickly.</p> <h3>Key Benefits of Our Security Services</h3> <ul class="benefits-list"> <li>Professional crowd control and security guard patrols</li> <li>VIP protection and executive security services</li> <li>Comprehensive emergency evacuation planning</li> <li>Access control management with entry screening</li> <li>Rapid incident response and conflict resolution</li> <li>Baggage and personal item screening services</li> <li>Emergency medical coordination and planning</li> <li>Full compliance with Australian safety regulations</li> </ul> <p>We work closely with corporate organisations to deliver <a href="corporatesecurity.html" style="color: var(--primary); text-decoration: underline;">corporate security solutions</a> for annual general meetings, product launches, shareholder events and awards evenings. Our <a href="alarmresponses.html" style="color: var(--primary); text-decoration: underline;">24/7 alarm response services</a> also support venues during overnight setup periods, post-event lockdowns and out-of-hours access so the building remains protected even when the event is over.</p> </div> </div> </section> <!-- Service Features Section --> <section class="service-features"> <div Mobile Patrols?</h3> <p>Mobile patrols involve trained mobile patrol officers conducting regular and random inspections of properties using clearly marked mobile patrol vehicles. This service provides a strong deterrent presence while ensuring issues are identified and addressed quickly.</p> <p>At Broadsafe Services, our mobile patrol units carry out roving patrols, vehicle checks and site inspections in line with agreed patrol routes. Our officers respond promptly to incidents, alarms and security concerns, ensuring consistent protection across single or multiple locations.</p> <h3>Key Benefits</h3> <ul class="benefits-list"> <li>Random patrol schedules to reduce predictability</li> <li>Highly visible mobile patrol security guards</li> <li>Thorough property inspections with clear reporting</li> <li>Rapid response to alarms and incidents</li> <li>Cost-effective protection for multiple sites</li> <li>Strong deterrent against unauthorised activity</li> <li>24/7 coverage options, including overnight monitoring</li> <li>Flexible patrol frequency to suit operational needs</li> </ul> </div> </div> </section> <!-- Service Features Section --> <section class="service-features"> <div class="section-title"> <h2>Our This visible security presence acts as a strong deterrent while ensuring immediate incident response when required.</p> <p>At <a href="https://www.broadsafeservices.com.au">Broadsafe Services</a>, our static guards are carefully selected, fully licensed and trained to carry out guard duties in line with site-specific requirements. Each deployment is based on a detailed assessment to ensure effective site protection and risk prevention.</p> <h3>Key Benefits</h3> <ul class="benefits-list"> <li>24/7 on-site static security guard presence</li> <li>Controlled access and visitor management</li> <li>Immediate response to incidents and emergencies</li> <li>Scheduled premises patrols and fixed post security</li> <li>Clear reporting and incident documentation</li> <li>Enhanced personnel safety and asset monitoring</li> <li>Reduced risk of theft, damage, or unauthorised access</li> <li>Tailored guarding plans based on site requirements</li> </ul> </div> </div> </section> <!-- Service Features Section --> <section class="service-features"> <div class="section-title"> <h2>Our Static Guarding Features</h2> <p>Practical, for (let cookie of cookies) { const [cookieName, cookieValue] = cookie.trim.split('='); if (cookieName === name) return cookieValue; } return null; } // ====== THEME TOGGLE ====== const themeToggle = document.createElement('button'); document.body.classList.toggle('nav-open', isOpen); if (mobileMenuBtn) { mobileMenuBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen? 'true': 'false'); } } if (!window.__mobileNavInitialized) { window.__mobileNavInitialized = true; if (mobileMenuBtn && mobileNav) { mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleMobileMenu); } if (mobileNavClose && mobileNav) { mobileNavClose.addEventListener('click', toggleMobileMenu); } // Close mobile menu when clicking on a link document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-nav a').forEach(link => { link.addEventListener('click', toggleMobileMenu); }); } // ====== HEADER SCROLL EFFECT ====== window.addEventListener('scroll', function { const header = document.querySelector('header'); if (window.scrollY > 50) { header.style.padding = '25px 5%'; // Grows to 110px total (80px + 50px padding) header.style.height = '80px'; // Maintain fixed height header.style.boxShadow = '0 5px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)'; } else { header.style.padding = '20px 5%'; // Default: 80px total (80px + 40px padding) header.style.height = '80px'; header.style.boxShadow = '0 2px 15px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)'; } }); // ====== WINDOW RESIZE HANDLER ====== window.addEventListener('resize', function { // Close mobile menu on resize to desktop if (window.innerWidth > 768 && mobileNav && mobileNav.classList.contains('is-open')) { toggleMobileMenu; } }); // ====== FAQ ACCORDION ====== const faqItems = document.querySelectorAll('.faq-item'); faqItems.forEach(item => { const question = item.classList.toggle('active'); answer.classList.toggle('active'); }); }); // ====== SMOOTH SCROLLING ====== document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
